# Converge Phase 1 projects

## User
**Timestamp:** 2026-07-21T18:21:55.154Z

# PHASE 1 CROSS-PROJECT CONVERGENCE

## Project One Voyage, Project Wayfarer, and Project Sealed Hold

Integrate the three completed Phase 1 implementation candidates into one coherent canonical architecture.

This is a dedicated convergence task.

Do not continue development directly on any source project branch.

Do not merge any candidate directly into `main`.

Do not begin Phase 2 of any project.

## Frozen candidate commits

Treat these exact commits as immutable integration inputs:

```text
Project One Voyage
Branch: integration/lanternwake-phase5-universal-language
Commit: 4e8f385687b01aa6b1e97452ff76e6e7e3b58b8c

Project Wayfarer
Branch: codex/project-wayfarer-phase1-unified-identity
Commit: a478d7957e112c9ce6f63fd423746d3df2a697ce

Project Sealed Hold
Branch: codex/project-sealed-hold-phase1
Commit: 4b93b4f4554ba504bec6d6462d39960dd28b4afe

Current reported origin/main:
0ecd2f9cca6116e2f7f9ab4408ade749fb061e72
```

Do not assume the reported `origin/main` is still current. Fetch and verify it.

---

# 1. Preflight and Baseline Selection

Before creating the convergence branch:

1. Fetch all remote branches.
2. Record all candidate commits and verify they exist.
3. Inspect the commit graph.
4. Determine the merge base of every candidate.
5. Determine exactly what commit `a0a2111c`, the reported One Voyage base, contains.
6. Identify whether the One Voyage branch includes accepted Lanternwake Phase 5 and Universal Language integration not present in `origin/main`.
7. Compare the candidate histories against current `origin/main`.
8. Select the correct convergence baseline based on accepted project history, not merely the newest timestamp or branch name.
9. Document the decision.

Create a new dedicated branch and worktree such as:

```text
codex/phase1-cross-project-convergence
../Forever-Treasure-Phase1-Convergence
```

The canonical checkout must remain untouched.

Do not modify the three source candidate branches.

---

# 2. Required Convergence Documents

Create:

```text
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Convergence_Design_Record.md
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Migration_Order.md
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Conflict_Ledger.csv
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Test_Plan.md
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Validation_Record.md
Development_Docs/Phase_1_Cross_Project_Integration_Manifest.txt
```

The design record must freeze:

* canonical Chronicle domain;
* canonical account domain;
* canonical Player profile relationship;
* canonical Creator and Captain actor relations;
* canonical authorization;
* canonical session and membership relationships;
* canonical audit ownership;
* canonical private-package relationship;
* canonical private-asset authorization;
* retained compatibility boundaries;
* final migration order.

---

# 3. Integration Order

Use this conceptual order:

1. Project One Voyage canonical content/runtime foundation.
2. Project Wayfarer canonical identity and actor ownership.
3. Project Sealed Hold private package, storage, import/export, and protected asset system.

Do not perform three blind merges.

For each candidate:

1. inspect its full diff;
2. identify overlapping files and concepts;
3. record conflicts in the conflict ledger;
4. choose the final architecture;
5. adapt source changes where required;
6. preserve candidate provenance;
7. run focused validation before continuing.

Merges, cherry-picks, or manual application may be used, but Git’s automatic conflict resolution is not the architecture decision.

---

# 4. Prisma and Migration Reconciliation

Reconcile all SQLite and MySQL schema changes under one migration sequence.

Known candidate migration identifiers include:

```text
Wayfarer SQLite:
20260721120000_wayfarer_unified_identity

Wayfarer MySQL:
0005_wayfarer_unified_identity

Sealed Hold SQLite:
20260721130000_project_sealed_hold_phase1

Sealed Hold MySQL:
0005_project_sealed_hold_phase1
```

The duplicate MySQL `0005` identifiers must be resolved deliberately.

Before changing migration identifiers, determine:

* whether any candidate migration has been applied outside disposable test databases;
* how the migration ledger tracks filenames and checksums;
* whether deployment scripts reference the identifiers;
* whether documentation references them;
* whether migration ordering depends on lexical or numeric order.

The final conceptual order must be:

1. canonical One Voyage domain migrations;
2. Wayfarer unified-account models;
3. Wayfarer identity and actor backfills;
4. Sealed Hold package/import/private-asset models;
5. cross-project foreign keys, constraints, and indexes;
6. compatibility deprecation changes.

Do not drop legacy tables during convergence unless already proven safe and explicitly required.

Additive compatibility is preferred for this integration release.

Test the final migration chain against:

* an empty SQLite database;
* a representative current SQLite database;
* legacy Campaign data;
* Player-only identity;
* Game Master-only identity;
* explicit identity match;
* ambiguous identity candidate;
* invitations and memberships;
* canonical Creator and Captain ownership;
* synthetic private-package data;
* an isolated MySQL schema;
* rerun/idempotency scenarios where supported.

---

# 5. Canonical Cross-Project Invariants

The final system must enforce:

## Chronicle

* One canonical Chronicle/Tall Tale domain.
* One immutable published-version domain.
* One canonical Tale Session runtime.
* One canonical Tale Session Event history.
* One canonical snapshot builder.
* One canonical command path.
* No active legacy business writer.

## Identity

* One canonical UserAccount per claimed person.
* One Player profile per claimed account.
* Player, Captain, and Creator are roles/capabilities.
* Creator and Captain writes use canonical account foreign keys.
* Legacy strings are historical compatibility snapshots only.
* Ambiguous identities are never automatically merged.

## Private content

* Private packages reference canonical Chronicle content.
* Private import ownership references canonical accounts.
* Private assets authorize through canonical roles, membership, publication state, and reveal state.
* Import never automatically publishes, launches, invites, or grants Player access.
* Package secrets never enter logs or persistent browser storage.

## Compatibility

* Legacy Player links continue securely.
* Legacy invitations continue securely.
* Quartermaster routes invoke canonical Captain services.
* Retained legacy tables are compatibility-only.
* Every retained legacy component has a documented removal gate.

---

Do not retain duplicate implementations merely because both compile.

Particular attention is required for:

* account session resolution;

* Creator and Captain actor foreign keys;
* audit-event models;
* Tale ownership;
* invitation ownership;
* private asset authorization;
* Studio navigation;
* route-module exports;
* migration runners;
* package scripts.

If production Rive assets require a genuine project artifact not available in the repository, document the exact external artifact requirement and keep release acceptance separate from implementation integration. Still commit and push the convergence candidate.

---

# 10. Cross-Project Acceptance Journeys

Add integrated tests proving:

1. One canonical account can access Player, Captain, and Creator surfaces.
2. That account creates a canonical Chronicle.
3. Creator ownership uses the canonical account.
4. A Captain starts a canonical Tale Session.
5. Captain ownership uses the canonical account.
6. A Player joins through a legacy-compatible invitation.
7. Guest claiming preserves membership.
8. Guest merging resolves duplicate membership safely.
9. The Creator exports the Chronicle as an encrypted private package.
10. The package round-trip verifies.
11. The package imports as a private draft.
12. Import creates no publication, session, invitation, or Player access.
13. An unauthorized Player cannot access imported assets.
14. A properly revealed asset becomes accessible to an authorized member.
15. Revoking membership removes access.
16. Restart preserves Chronicle, identity, membership, and private-content state.
17. Legacy writers remain untouched after canonical mutations.
18. No private sentinel appears in public output or unauthorized responses.

---

# 11. Validation

Run focused validation throughout integration.

Before final acceptance run:

* formatting;
* lint;
* TypeScript;
* Prisma formatting and validation;
* Prisma generation;
* SQLite migration rehearsal;
* live isolated MySQL migration/runtime proof;
* One Voyage migration/parity tests;
* Wayfarer lifecycle/reconciliation tests;
* Sealed Hold package/storage/import/export/backup tests;
* authorization and privacy tests;
* browser acceptance;
* restart proof;
* repository scan;
* staged-diff scan;
* production build;
* public-build sentinel scan;
* Lanternwake asset validation;
* full repository validation.

Record exact commands, environments, pass/fail/skip totals, ports, and database identities.

A skipped test is not a pass.

An unrelated failure must be classified accurately, but it must not prevent committing and pushing the durable convergence candidate.

---

# 12. Commit and Push Policy

Commit durable integration work throughout the convergence task.

A commit and push do not imply acceptance or merge approval.

At final checkpoint:

1. inspect the diff;
2. scan the exact staged changes;
3. create the final integration manifest;
4. compute its SHA-256;
5. commit all intended convergence work;
6. push the dedicated convergence branch;
7. report its exact commit hash.

Do not merge into `main`.

If all gates pass, mark the convergence candidate ready for owner acceptance.

If an external artifact or environment gate remains, mark it as a pushed blocked-acceptance candidate, not as nonexistent work.

Do not leave convergence only as uncommitted local changes.

---

# 13. Final Report

Report:

* selected baseline and rationale;
* source candidate hashes;
* convergence branch;
* ending commit;
* push result;
* schema decisions;
* migration order;
* conflicts resolved;
* files changed;
* tests added;
* pass/fail/skip totals;
* SQLite proof;
* MySQL proof;
* browser proof;
* restart proof;
* private-content proof;
* scanner proof;
* remaining blockers;
* retained compatibility;
* exact removal gates;
* integration-manifest SHA-256.

Stop after pushing the convergence branch.

Do not merge into `main`.

Do not start Harborlight or any Phase 2.

if (folded.has(key)) return true; folded.add(key); return false; }) || paths.length > privateLimits().fileCount) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_PATH_REJECTED\");\n  let size = 0;\n  for (const entryPath of normalized) {\n    const bytes = Buffer.from(payload.entries[entryPath] ?? \"\", \"base64url\"); size += bytes.length;\n    if (bytes.length > privateLimits().assetBytes || payload.checksums[entryPath] !== sha256(bytes)) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_CHECKSUM_MISMATCH\");\n  }\n  if (size > privateLimits().plaintextBytes || manifest.totals.files !== paths.length || manifest.totals.assets !== manifest.assets.length || manifest.totals.plaintextBytes !== size) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_LIMIT_EXCEEDED\");\n  for (const tale of manifest.tales) if (!payload.entries[assertSafeArchivePath(tale.contentPath)]) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_INVALID\");\n  const logicalAssets = new Set<string>();\n  const approvedMedia: Record<PrivatePackageManifest[\"assets\"][number][\"representation\"], RegExp> = {\n    image: /^image\\/(?:avif|gif|jpeg|png|webp)$/,\n    audio: /^audio\\/(?:mpeg|ogg|wav)$/,\n    video: /^video\\/(?:mp4|webm)$/,\n    document: /^application\\/pdf$/,\n    \"model-3d\": /^(?:model\\/gltf-binary|model\\/gltf\\+json)$/,\n    binary: /^application\\/octet-stream$/,\n  };\n  for (const asset of manifest.assets) {\n    if (logicalAssets.has(asset.logicalId) || !approvedMedia[asset.representation].test(asset.mediaType)) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_INVALID\");\n    logicalAssets.add(asset.logicalId);\n    const bytes = Buffer.from(payload.entries[assertSafeArchivePath(asset.relativePath)] ?? \"\", \"base64url\");\n    const expectedMagic = asset.representation === \"image\" && asset.mediaType === \"image/png\" ? Buffer.from([0x89, 0x50, 0x4e, 0x47]) : asset.representation === \"document\" ? Buffer.from(\"%PDF-\") : asset.representation === \"model-3d\" ? Buffer.from(\"glTF\") : undefined;\n    if (!bytes.length || bytes.length !== asset.byteLength || sha256(bytes) !== asset.sha256 || (expectedMagic && !bytes.subarray(0, expectedMagic.length).equals(expectedMagic))) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_CHECKSUM_MISMATCH\");\n  }\n  return manifest;\n}\n\nexport function makePayload(input: Omit<PrivatePayload, \"checksums\">): PrivatePayload {\n  const checksums = Object.fromEntries(Object.entries(input.entries).map(([key, value]) => [key, sha256(Buffer.from(value, \"base64url\"))]));\n  const payload = { ...input, checksums }; validatePayload(payload); return payload;\n}\n\n===== src/private-content/service.ts =====\r\nimport { randomUUID } from \"node:crypto\";\nimport { mkdir, writeFile } from src/private-content/security.ts =====\r\nimport { readdir, readFile } from \"node:fs/promises\";\nimport path from \"node:path\";\nimport { PRIVATE_SENTINEL } from \"./core\";\n\nconst forbiddenPath = [/\\.ftprivate$/i, /\\.ftkey$/i, /(^|[\\\\/])(?:private-content|private-exports|decrypted-private-content)([\\\\/]|$)/i];\nconst forbiddenContent = [/aws_secret_access_key\\s*=\\s*\\S+/i, new RegExp(PRIVATE_SENTINEL)];\nconst pemPrivateKey = /-----BEGIN (?:RSA |OPENSSH |EC )?PRIVATE KEY-----\\s*(?:[A-Za-z0-9+/]{20,}={0,2}\\s*)+-----END (?:RSA |OPENSSH |EC )?PRIVATE KEY-----/m;\nasync function walk(root: string, files: string[] = []): Promise<string[]> { for (const entry of await readdir(root, { withFileTypes: true })) { if ([\".git\", \"node_modules\", \".next\"].includes(entry.name) || entry.name.startsWith(\".sealed-build\")) continue; const candidate = path.join(root, entry.name); if (entry.isDirectory()) await walk(candidate, files); else files.push(candidate); } return files; }\nexport async function scanPrivateContent(root = process.cwd()) { const hits: Array<{ path: string; rule: string }> = []; for (const file of await walk(root)) forbiddenPath.find((rule) => rule.test(relative)); if (nameRule) { hits.push({ path: relative, rule: \"forbidden-path\" }); continue; } if (/\\.(?:ts|tsx|js|json|md|env|txt)$/i.test(file)) { const function scanBuildOutput(root = process.env.NEXT_DIST_DIR ? path.resolve(process.cwd(), process.env.NEXT_DIST_DIR, \"static\") : path.join(process.cwd(), \".next\", \"static\")) {\n  try {\n    const \"node:fs/promises\";\nimport path from \"node:path\";\nimport { randomUUID } from \"node:crypto\";\nimport { isWithin, privateFailure, sha256 } from \"./core\";\n\nexport type StagedPrivateObject = { stagingId: string; sha256: string; byteLength: number };\nexport type StoredPrivateObject = { sha256: string; storageKey: string; byteLength: number };\n\nfunction safeConfiguredRoot(value: string | undefined, label: string) {\n  if (!value || !path.isAbsolute(value)) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_CONTENT_CONFIGURATION_INVALID\", `${label} is not configured securely.`);\n  const resolved = path.resolve(value); const repository = path.resolve(process.cwd());\n  const forbidden = [repository, path.join(repository, \"public\"), path.join(repository, \".next\"), path.join(repository, \"src\")];\n  if (forbidden.some((candidate) => isWithin(candidate, resolved) || isWithin(resolved, candidate))) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_CONTENT_CONFIGURATION_INVALID\", `${label} is not configured securely.`);\n  return resolved;\n}\n\nexport class LocalPrivateAssetStore {\n  readonly root: string; readonly stagingRoot: string;\n  constructor(input: { root?: string; stagingRoot?: string } = {}) {\n    this.root = safeConfiguredRoot(input.root ?? process.env.PRIVATE_CONTENT_ROOT, \"Private content storage\");\n    this.stagingRoot = safeConfiguredRoot(input.stagingRoot ?? process.env.PRIVATE_CONTENT_STAGING_ROOT, \"Private content staging\");\n    if (this.root === this.stagingRoot) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_CONTENT_CONFIGURATION_INVALID\", \"Private storage roots must be distinct.\");\n  }\n  private objectPath(hash: string) {\n    if (!/^[a-f0-9]{64}$/.test(hash)) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_INVALID\");\n    return path.join(this.root, \"objects\", hash.slice(0, 2), hash.slice(2, 4), hash);\n  }\n  async stageObject(buffer: Buffer, expectedSha256 = sha256(buffer)): Promise<StagedPrivateObject> {\n    if (sha256(buffer) !== expectedSha256) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_CHECKSUM_MISMATCH\");\n    const stagingId = randomUUID(); const directory = path.join(this.stagingRoot, stagingId); const target = path.join(directory, expectedSha256);\n    await mkdir(directory, { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 }); await writeFile(target, buffer, { flag: \"wx\", mode: 0o600 });\n    return { stagingId, sha256: expectedSha256, byteLength: buffer.length };\n  }\n  async finalizeObject(staged: StagedPrivateObject): Promise<StoredPrivateObject> {\n    const source = path.join(this.stagingRoot, staged.stagingId, staged.sha256); const destination = this.objectPath(staged.sha256);\n    const bytes = await readFile(source); if (bytes.length !== staged.byteLength || sha256(bytes) !== staged.sha256) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_CHECKSUM_MISMATCH\");\n    await mkdir(path.dirname(destination), { recursive: true, mode: 0o700 });\n    try { await rename(source, destination); } catch (error: unknown) {\n      if (!(error && typeof error === \"object\" && \"code\" in error && (error as { code?: string }).code === \"EEXIST\")) throw error;\n      const existing = await readFile(destination); if (existing.length !== staged.byteLength || sha256(existing) !== staged.sha256) throw privateFailure(\"PRIVATE_PACKAGE_CONFLICT\");\n    }\n    await this.deleteStagedObject(staged.stagingId);\n    return { sha256: staged.sha256, storageKey: `objects/${staged.sha256.slice(0, 2)}/${staged.sha256.slice(2, 4)}/${staged.sha256}`, byteLength: staged.byteLength };\n  }\n  async objectExists(hash: string) { try { await access(this.objectPath(hash)); return true; } catch { return false; } }\n  async verifyObject(hash: string) { try { const bytes = await readFile(this.objectPath(hash)); return { exists: true, valid: sha256(bytes) === hash, byteLength: bytes.length }; } catch { return { exists: false, valid: false, byteLength: 0 }; } }\n  async readObject(hash: string) { return readFile(this.objectPath(hash)); }\n  readObjectStream(hash: string) { return createReadStream(this.objectPath(hash)); }\n  async deleteStagedObject(stagingId: string) { if (!/^[a-f0-9-]{36}$/i.test(stagingId)) return; await rm(path.join(this.stagingRoot, stagingId), { recursive: true, force: true }); }\n  async deleteUnreferencedObject(hash: string) { await src/app/api/private-assets/[assetId]/route.ts =====\r\nimport { NextResponse } from \"next/server\";\nimport { privateContentAuthorization } from \"@/private-content/authorization\";\nimport { LocalPrivateAssetStore } from \"@/private-content/storage\";\nimport { db } from \"@/lib/db\";\n\nfunction rangeFor(header: string | null, length: number) {\n  if (!header) return null;\n  const match = /^bytes=(\\d*)-(\\d*)$/.exec(header);\n  if (!match) return false;\n  const start = match[1] ? Number(match[1]) : Math.max(0, length - Number(match[2]));\n  const end = match[2] ? Number(match[2]) : length - 1;\n  if (!Number.isSafeInteger(start) || !Number.isSafeInteger(end) || start < 0 || end < start || start >= length) return false;\n  return { start, end: Math.min(end, length - 1) };\n}\n\nexport async function GET(request: Request, context: { params: Promise<{ assetId: string }> }) {\n  try {\n    const assetId = (await context.params).assetId;\n    const playthroughId = new URL(request.url).searchParams.get(\"playthrough\");\n    if (!(await privateContentAuthorization.canReadPrivateAsset({ assetId, playthroughId }))) throw new Error(\"not-found\");\n    const reference = await db.privateAssetReference.findFirst({ where: { id: assetId, available: true }, include: { object: true } });\n    if (!reference) throw new Error(\"not-found\");\n    const source = await new LocalPrivateAssetStore().readObject(reference.object.sha256);\n    const range = rangeFor(request.headers.get(\"range\"), source.length);\n    if (range === false) return new Response(null, { status: 416, headers: { \"Content-Range\": `bytes */${source.length}`, \"Cache-Control\": \"private, no-store\" } });\n    const body = range ? source.subarray(range.start, range.end + 1) : source;\n    return new Response(body, {\n      status: range ? 206 : 200,\n      headers: {\n        \"Content-Type\": reference.object.mediaType,\n        \"Content-Length\": String(body.length),\n        \"Accept-Ranges\": \"bytes\",\n        ...(range ?
